###### ↳ ↳ ↳ Re: Cross-language challenge (of POSSIBLE interest)

- **From:** "Rick Smith" <ricksmith@mfi.net>
- **Date:** 2005-02-24T15:00:53-05:00
- **Newsgroups:** comp.lang.cobol
- **Message-ID:** `<111scngmtq9s446@corp.supernews.com>`
- **References:** `<G1PPd.2059185$f47.360893@news.easynews.com> <111q4nm73lgvk8c@corp.supernews.com> <e2927$421e148b$45491f85$5170@KNOLOGY.NET>`

```

"LX-i" <lxi0007@netscape.net> wrote in message
news:e2927$421e148b$45491f85$5170@KNOLOGY.NET...
> Rick Smith wrote:
> >
…[6 more quoted lines elided]…
> to learn...

This is the subprogram that implemented the binary tree. This is not
the same solution used for the ANSI 85 conforming program.

      $set optspeed noalter notrickle noparamcountcheck
       identification division.
       program-id. bin-tree.
       data division.
       working-storage section.
       01 heap-id pic x(2) comp-5.
       01 status-word pic x(2).
       01 deepest-probe pic x(2) comp-5 value 0.
       01 probe-depth pic x(2) comp-5.
       01 number-of-probes pic x(4) comp-5 value 0.
       01 sum-of-levels pic x(4) comp-5 value 0.
       01 stats-display.
         02 pic x value space.
         02 deepest-probe-display pic zzz9.
         02 pic x value space.
         02 average-probe-display pic zzz9.9.
         02 pic x(6) value space.
       01 root-ptr pic x(4) comp-5.
       01 node-ptr pic x(4) comp-5.
       01 new-node-ptr pic x(4) comp-5 value 0.
       01 node-size pic x(4) comp-5 value 32.
       01 flags pic x(4) comp-5 value 0.
       01 status-code pic x(2) comp-5.
       01 node.
         02 l-node-ptr pic x(4) comp-5.
         02 key-field pic x(18).
         02  pic x(2).
         02 r-node-ptr pic x(4) comp-5.
         02  pic x(4).
       01 new-node.
         02 new-l-node-ptr pic x(4) comp-5.
         02 new-key-field pic x(18).
         02  pic x(2).
         02 new-r-node-ptr pic x(4) comp-5.
         02  pic x(4).
       linkage section.
       01 insert-status pic x.
         88 init value "i".
         88 clean-up value "c".
         88 failure value "0".
         88 success value "1".
       01 word-text pic x(18).
       procedure division using insert-status word-text.
       begin section.
           if clean-up
               call "CBL_CLOSE_VFILE" using by value heap-id
                 returning status-code
               move deepest-probe to deepest-probe-display
               compute average-probe-display =
                   sum-of-levels / number-of-probes
               move stats-display to word-text
               exit program
           end-if
           if init
               move 0 to root-ptr
               move 0 to node-ptr
               call "CBL_OPEN_VFILE" using heap-id status-word
                 returning status-code
           end-if
           if root-ptr = 0
               perform init-new-node
               move new-node-ptr to root-ptr
               set success to true
               exit program
           end-if
           move root-ptr to node-ptr
           move 0 to probe-depth
           add 1 to number-of-probes
           perform until exit
               add 1 to probe-depth
               perform read-node
               if key-field = word-text
                   set failure to true
                   exit perform
               end-if
               if word-text < key-field
                   if l-node-ptr = 0
                       perform init-new-node
                       move new-node-ptr to l-node-ptr
                       perform write-node
                       set success to true
                       exit perform
                   end-if
                   move l-node-ptr to node-ptr
                   exit perform cycle
               end-if
               if word-text > key-field
                   if r-node-ptr = 0
                       perform init-new-node
                       move new-node-ptr to r-node-ptr
                       perform write-node
                       set success to true
                       exit perform
                   end-if
                   move r-node-ptr to node-ptr
                   exit perform cycle
               end-if
           end-perform
           add probe-depth to sum-of-levels
           if probe-depth > deepest-probe
               move probe-depth to deepest-probe
           end-if
           exit program
           .
       init-new-node section.
           add node-size to new-node-ptr
           move spaces to new-node
           move 0 to new-l-node-ptr
           move 0 to new-r-node-ptr
           move word-text to new-key-field
           call "CBL_WRITE_VFILE" using by value heap-id
               new-node-ptr node-size by reference new-node
             returning status-code
           if status-code not = 0
               set failure to true
               exit program
           end-if
           .
       read-node section.
           call "CBL_READ_VFILE" using by value heap-id
               node-ptr node-size by reference node
             returning status-code
           if status-code not = 0
               set failure to true
               exit program
           end-if
           .
       write-node section.
           call "CBL_WRITE_VFILE" using by value heap-id
               node-ptr node-size by reference node
             returning status-code
           if status-code not = 0
               set failure to true
               exit program
           end-if
           .
       end program bin-tree.
```
